### 1C Enterprise
```1C Enterprise
a!localVariables(
  local!listOfMap: {
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

### 2-Dimensional Array
```2-Dimensional Array
a!localVariables(
  local!listOfMap: {
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

### AsciiDoc
```AsciiDoc
a!localVariables(
  local!listOfMap: {
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

```AspectJ
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

```Assembly
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

```Astro
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

```Asymptote
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

```Mako
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

### Markdown
```Markdown
a!localVariables(
  local!listOfMap: {
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
```

```Marko
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

```Mask
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),

    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

```Mathematica
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

### SELinux Policy
```SELinux Policy
a!localVariables(
  local!listOfMap: {
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
```

```SMT
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

### TextMate Properties
```TextMate Properties
a!localVariables(
  local!listOfMap: {
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
```

```Yul
  local!listOfMap: {
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```

### ZAP
```ZAP
a!localVariables(
  local!listOfMap: {
    a!map(id: 1, value: a!map(subValue: "first map")),
    a!map(id: 2, value: "second map"),
    a!map(id: 3, value: "third map"),
    a!map(id: 4, value: a!map(subValue: "fourth map")),
    a!map(id: 5, value: "fifth map"),
    a!map(id: 6, value: "sixth map"),
  },
  
  a!map(
    one: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap),
    unique3: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 3, true),
    ten: fn!spt_list_randomelement(local!listOfMap, 10)
  )
)
```
